	<div class="wpb_raw_code wpb_raw_js" >
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" href="//cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/slick-carousel@1.8.1/slick/slick.css"/>
<script type="text/javascript" src="//cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/slick-carousel@1.8.1/slick/slick.min.js"></script>
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function(){
    //Add Active to tab on page load
    $panels = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-panels .vc_tta-panel');
    $tabs = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-list .vc_tta-tab');
    var index = 0;

    //Align Tabs with panels
    $panels.each(function(){
        jQuery(this).hasClass('vc_active');
        return false;
        index++;
    })
    var newIndex = 0;
    $tabs.each(function(){
        if(index == newIndex){
            jQuery(this).addClass('vc_active');
        }
        newIndex++;
    })

    //Add custom icon to tabs
    var iconIndex = 1;
    $panels.each(function(){
        $this = jQuery(this);
        $tab = $this.find('.tab-icon');
        $tab.find('img').prependTo(jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tab:nth-of-type(' + iconIndex + ') a'));
        jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tab:nth-of-type(' + iconIndex + ') a i').remove()
        $tab.remove();
        iconIndex++;
    })
});
jQuery(window).on('load resize orientationchange', function() {
    var $carousel = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-container .vc_tta-tabs-list');
    var $click = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-container .vc_tta-tabs-list .vc_tta-tab');

    //Change slide to selected panel for tabs
    var slideGoTo = function(){
        if ($carousel.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
            $carousel.slick('slickGoTo', +jQuery(this).attr('data-slick-index'));
            setTimeout(function(){ 
                $click = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-container .vc_tta-tabs-list .vc_tta-tab');
                $click.each(function(){
                    if(jQuery(this).hasClass('vc_active') && (!jQuery(this).hasClass('slick-center') || !jQuery(this).hasClass('slick-active'))){
                        jQuery(this).removeClass('vc_active');
                    }
                })
            }, 1000);
        }
    }

    //Update panel for selected slide (aka tab)
    var afterChangeFunction = function(slick, currentSlide){
        $currentTab = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-container .vc_tta-tabs-list .vc_tta-tab.slick-center.slick-active a');
        if(!$currentTab.parent().hasClass('vc_active')){
            $currentTab.trigger('click');
        }
        /*setTimeout(function(){ 
            $click = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-container .vc_tta-tabs-list .vc_tta-tab');
            $click.each(function(){
                if(jQuery(this).hasClass('vc_active') && (!jQuery(this).hasClass('slick-center') || !jQuery(this).hasClass('slick-active'))){
                    jQuery(this).removeClass('vc_active');
                }
            })
        }, 1000);*/
    }

    /* Initializes a slick carousel only on mobile screens */
    // slick on mobile
    if (jQuery(window).width() > 768) {
        if ($carousel.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
            $carousel.slick('unslick');
            $click = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-container .vc_tta-tabs-list .vc_tta-tab');
            $click.unbind('click', slideGoTo)
            $carousel.unbind('afterChange', afterChangeFunction);
        }
    }
    else{
        if (!$carousel.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
            $carousel.slick({
                slidesToShow: 3,
                slidesToScroll: 1,
                mobileFirst: true,
                infinite: true,
                centerMode: true,
                centerPadding: '50px'
            });
            $click = jQuery('.cybv2_customer_stories_tabs .vc_tta-tabs-container .vc_tta-tabs-list .vc_tta-tab');
            $click.bind('click', slideGoTo)
            $carousel.bind('afterChange', afterChangeFunction);
            $click.each(function(){
                if(jQuery(this).hasClass('vc_active') && !jQuery(this).hasClass('slick-cloned')){
                    jQuery(this).trigger('click');
                }
            })
        }
    }
});
</script>

			<script>
	jQuery('.cybv2_resources_uberflip').on('DOMSubtreeModified', function(){
		//Get tiles
		$tiles = jQuery('.cybv2_resources_uberflip .tile.single');
		var updated = false;
		//Make sure tiles exist
		if($tiles.length > 0){
			var allAvailable = true;
			//Check if all tiles loaded in
			jQuery.each($tiles, function( index, elem ) {
				$tile = jQuery(elem);
				if($tile.find('.ob-custom-label').html() == undefined && $tile.attr('id') != 'loading-notifier'){
					allAvailable = false;
				}
			});
			//Check if loaded in
			if(allAvailable){
				jQuery.each($tiles, function( index, elem ) {
					$tile = jQuery(elem);
					var updated = false;
					//Check if tile to update
					if($tile.find('.ob-custom-label').html() != undefined && $tile.data('updated') == undefined){
						jQuery('.cybv2_resources_uberflip').off('DOMSubtreeModified');
						$tags = $tile.data('tags').split(',');

						//Grab tag
						$tag = $tile.find('.ob-custom-label').html();

						//Check tags and change link accordingly
						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'analyst-report'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Download Analyst Report');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'blog'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Read Blog');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'case-study'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Download Case Study');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'ebook'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').css('text-transform', 'none');
							$tile.find('.ob-custom-label').css('text-transform', 'none');
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Download eBook');
							$tag = $tile.find('.ob-custom-label').html('eBook');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'infographic'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Download Infographic');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'webinar'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Watch Webinar');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'product-datasheet'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Download Product Datasheet');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'solution-brief'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Download Solution Brief');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'video'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Watch Video');
						}

						if(string_to_slug($tag) == 'whitepaper'){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Download Whitepaper');
						}

						if($tile.hasClass('blogpost')){
							$tile.find('.item-link.view').html('Read Blog');
						}

						if(updated == false){
							updated = true;
							$tile.data('updated', true);
						}
					}
				});
			}
		}
	});

	function string_to_slug (str) {
		if (typeof str === 'string' || str instanceof String){
			str = str.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, ''); // trim
		    str = str.toLowerCase();
		  
		    // remove accents, swap  for n, etc
		    var from = "/_,:;";
		    var to   = "aaaaeeeeiiiioooouuuunc------";
		    for (var i=0, l=from.length ; i<l ; i++) {
		        str = str.replace(new RegExp(from.charAt(i), 'g'), to.charAt(i));
		    }

		    str = str.replace(/[^a-z0-9 -]/g, '') // remove invalid chars
		        .replace(/\s+/g, '-') // collapse whitespace and replace by -
		        .replace(/-+/g, '-'); // collapse dashes
		}

	    return str;
	}
</script>
